Location: 14 minutes to Vientiane, 20-25 minutes to Dongguan Street, which is definitely far in Yangzhou.

Environment: next to government agencies, quiet but not prosperous. Next to it is Sansheng, an old shopping center.

Problem: The design of the room is very, very, very unreasonable. The bathroom floor is very slippery. It should be that someone often slips and falls. I myself slipped and fell by the pool on the first day of my stay and broke my leg. The next day the family fell in the same place and hit their fingers! This was after putting an extra bath towel immediately after a fall. The main problem is the design of the bathroom space. The doors of the shower and the toilet are opened outwards, giving people a small space and WeChat, and the bathroom is uncomfortable overall. It is a tofu project!

Room: The convenient hotel is not as good as the whole season. Not like a Hilton hotel. Not even as good as Huan Peng.

Service: don't expect much service. 1. The welcome fruit is either placed in the house or a bag is stuffed in your hand when you settle in, like a garbage bag. 2. After the fall, the manager came to get a big medicine box and a bunch of ice cubes. You have ice packs. The gauze is the kind of slender gauze that can't hold things and doesn't know how to get ice cubes. 3. At 6 o'clock in the morning, the next room of the hotel starts to play music in an infinite loop, which is very noisy. I called the hotel but didn't answer, and there was no one after waiting for 20 minutes. In the end, it was because the room next door was not checked after checking out, and the alarm clock used by the last customer rang! The whole experience couldn't have been worse.

Originally, there were Mercure and Novetel in the city center with better prices than here, but I decided to stay here mainly because I was worried that the street would be noisy. But from the hardware to the service, I experienced the experience of a small broken hotel in a fourth-tier city, and I paid for the Hilton double tree. It can be said that it is the worst double tree I have ever lived in. A word of advice, don't live!
